info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in February 2024

posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:Warm and vibrant Westin hotel. During the Spring Festival of the Year of the Dragon in 2024, I took my old mother and children to travel to Xiamen. When choosing a hotel on Ctrip, you need to be knowledgeable. Because I came here by plane instead of driving by car, several big-name hotels that I originally liked were excluded because they were far away from the city center. It was the Spring Festival there again, and it was too far to take a taxi when traveling, or the location was too remote to even take a taxi. In the end, I chose the well-reviewed 5-star Westin Hotel. The fare to Bashi, Zhongshan Road Pedestrian Street, the Botanical Garden, and the bookstore all cost more than 20 yuan, and there were many buses. The child had a fever and went to the Zhongshan Hospital Affiliated to Xiamen University. It is a 2.8-kilometer drive. You can order takeout at a very authentic store. There is an SM Plaza 2 kilometers away, where locals go to eat.
The hotel staff are warm and unpretentious, and their kindness radiates from the inside out. You don't need to tell me, the service staff will take care of you spontaneously. Sometimes, out of fear of embarrassing you, they will help you and then walk away as if nothing happened. Seeing that there were so many of us, we quietly refilled a few more bottles of mineral water, and added an extra bath towel and toothbrush. I was very moved when I saw these after I came back from playing in the evening.
 The hotel breakfast is great. So many people are quiet and orderly, enjoying all the delicacies, chatting, feeding the baby in the baby chair, whispering among lovers, everyone will slow down and be leisurely.
 There are many types of dishes, but they are not simply stacked, and the taste is very thoughtful. The shrimp and fish fillet porridge made by the chef on the spot is really delicious. The fish fillets are white and tender, and only the middle part of the shrimp is removed. The local sand tea noodles are also very popular. The bread also tastes freshly baked.
 The texture of the bedding is silk, hanging and soft. The mattress is soft but supportive. I like the long wooden table and big chairs in the room. Very comfortable to sit on.
 A good trip starts with choosing a good hotel.
